Reset value0x00000003

Mask:SENT_CLC_MASK = 0x0000003f
Masks:  SENT_CLC_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:SENT_CLC_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
DISR 1 0 - 0 rw 0x00000001 Module Disable Request Bit
DISS 1 1 - 1 r 0x00000002 Module Disable Status Bit
SPEN 1 2 - 2 rw 0x00000004 Module Suspend Enable for OCDS
EDIS 1 3 - 3 rw 0x00000008 Sleep Mode Enable Control
SBWE 1 4 - 4 w 0x00000010 Module Suspend Bit Write Enable for OCDS
FSOE 1 5 - 5 rw 0x00000020 Fast Switch Off Enable

SENT_FDR

"SENT Fractional Divider Register"

AddressSENT_FDR_ADDR = 0xF032100C
Absolute addressableNo
Reset value0x00000000
C typeSENT_FDR_t

SENT_FDR.bits "SENT Fractional Divider Register"
Mask:SENT_FDR_MASK = 0x03ffc7ff
Masks:  SENT_FDR_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:SENT_FDR_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
STEP 10 0 - 9 rw 0x000003ff Step Value
FDIS 1 10 - 10 rw 0x00000400 Freeze Disable
0 Module operates on corrected clock, with reduced modulation jitter (default)
1 Module operates on uncorrected clock with full modulation jitter
DM 2 14 - 15 rw 0x0000c000 Divider Mode
00 Fractional divider is switched off; no output clock is generated. The Reset External Divider signal is 1. RESULT is not updated (default after System Reset).
01 Normal Divider Mode selected.
10 Fractional Divider Mode selected.
11 Fractional divider is switched off; no output clock is generated. RESULT is not updated.
RESULT 10 16 - 25 rh 0x03ff0000 Result Value
 readable0x03ffc7ff 
writeable0x0000c7ff
volatile0x03ff0000

Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
CEN 1 0 - 0 rw 0x00000001 Channel Enable
0 channel x disabled (default)
1 channel x enabled
IEP 1 1 - 1 rw 0x00000002 Ignore End Pulse
0 End Pulse not ignored (default)
1 End Pulse ignored
ACE 1 2 - 2 rw 0x00000004 Alternative CRC Mode Enable
0 Serial CRC calculation as specified in J2716 FEB2008 Rev. 3 2009-06-24 (default)
1 Alternative: 4 bit in parallel CRC calculation as used e.g. in hall sensor TLE4998C.
SNI 1 3 - 3 rw 0x00000008 Status Nibble Included in CRC
0 Status Nibble not included in CRC (default)
1 Status Nibble included in CRC (as used e.g. in hall sensor TLE4998C).
SDP 1 4 - 4 rw 0x00000010 Serial Data Processing Mode
0 Automatic Serial Data Processing is disabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx for SW processing. (default)
1 Automatic Serial Data Processing is enabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx; Message ID, Serial Data and SCRC can be read from SDSx after serial data interrupt SDI is activated.
SCDIS 1 5 - 5 rw 0x00000020 CRC for Serial Data Disabled Mode
00 CRC is enabled (default)
01 CRC is disabled CRC nibble can be read from SDSx. The CPU must perform the CRC on the current data by SW.
CDIS 1 6 - 6 rw 0x00000040 CRC Disabled Mode
00 CRC is enabled (default)
01 CRC is disabled CRC nibble can be read from RSRx. The CPU must perform the CRC on the current data by SW.

0 Check against Past Sync Pulse
1 Check against Future Sync Pulse

Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
CEN 1 0 - 0 rw 0x00000001 Channel Enable
0 channel x disabled (default)
1 channel x enabled
IEP 1 1 - 1 rw 0x00000002 Ignore End Pulse
0 End Pulse not ignored (default)
1 End Pulse ignored
ACE 1 2 - 2 rw 0x00000004 Alternative CRC Mode Enable
0 Serial CRC calculation as specified in J2716 FEB2008 Rev. 3 2009-06-24 (default)
1 Alternative: 4 bit in parallel CRC calculation as used e.g. in hall sensor TLE4998C.
SNI 1 3 - 3 rw 0x00000008 Status Nibble Included in CRC
0 Status Nibble not included in CRC (default)
1 Status Nibble included in CRC (as used e.g. in hall sensor TLE4998C).
SDP 1 4 - 4 rw 0x00000010 Serial Data Processing Mode
0 Automatic Serial Data Processing is disabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx for SW processing. (default)
1 Automatic Serial Data Processing is enabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx; Message ID, Serial Data and SCRC can be read from SDSx after serial data interrupt SDI is activated.
SCDIS 1 5 - 5 rw 0x00000020 CRC for Serial Data Disabled Mode
00 CRC is enabled (default)
01 CRC is disabled CRC nibble can be read from SDSx. The CPU must perform the CRC on the current data by SW.
CDIS 1 6 - 6 rw 0x00000040 CRC Disabled Mode
00 CRC is enabled (default)
01 CRC is disabled CRC nibble can be read from RSRx. The CPU must perform the CRC on the current data by SW.

CEN 1 0 - 0 rw 0x00000001 Channel Enable
0 channel x disabled (default)
1 channel x enabled

0 End Pulse not ignored (default)
1 End Pulse ignored
ACE 1 2 - 2 rw 0x00000004 Alternative CRC Mode Enable
0 Serial CRC calculation as specified in J2716 FEB2008 Rev. 3 2009-06-24 (default)

0 Status Nibble not included in CRC (default)
1 Status Nibble included in CRC (as used e.g. in hall sensor TLE4998C).

0 Automatic Serial Data Processing is disabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx for SW processing. (default)
1 Automatic Serial Data Processing is enabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx; Message ID, Serial Data and SCRC can be read from SDSx after serial data interrupt SDI is activated.
SCDIS 1 5 - 5 rw 0x00000020 CRC for Serial Data Disabled Mode
00 CRC is enabled (default)
01 CRC is disabled CRC nibble can be read from SDSx. The CPU must perform the CRC on the current data by SW.

00 CRC is enabled (default)

CEN 1 0 - 0 rw 0x00000001 Channel Enable
0 channel x disabled (default)
1 channel x enabled
IEP 1 1 - 1 rw 0x00000002 Ignore End Pulse
0 End Pulse not ignored (default)
1 End Pulse ignored
ACE 1 2 - 2 rw 0x00000004 Alternative CRC Mode Enable
0 Serial CRC calculation as specified in J2716 FEB2008 Rev. 3 2009-06-24 (default)
1 Alternative: 4 bit in parallel CRC calculation as used e.g. in hall sensor TLE4998C.
SNI 1 3 - 3 rw 0x00000008 Status Nibble Included in CRC
0 Status Nibble not included in CRC (default)
1 Status Nibble included in CRC (as used e.g. in hall sensor TLE4998C).
SDP 1 4 - 4 rw 0x00000010 Serial Data Processing Mode
0 Automatic Serial Data Processing is disabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx for SW processing. (default)
1 Automatic Serial Data Processing is enabled. Status and Communication nibble can be read from RSRx; Message ID, Serial Data and SCRC can be read from SDSx after serial data interrupt SDI is activated.
SCDIS 1 5 - 5 rw 0x00000020 CRC for Serial Data Disabled Mode
00 CRC is enabled (default)
01 CRC is disabled CRC nibble can be read from SDSx. The CPU must perform the CRC on the current data by SW.
CDIS 1 6 - 6 rw 0x00000040 CRC Disabled Mode
00 CRC is enabled (default)
01 CRC is disabled CRC nibble can be read from RSRx. The CPU must perform the CRC on the current data by SW.
